## 2026-05-21 � Improvement Loop 4 � Open Bionics math-hygiene flag CLOSED as false positive

**Resolution:** The 18-cycle "math-hygiene CRITICAL BLOCKING" flag on Open Bionics (and by extension 12 sibling robotics-labs entities Ottobock, Apexica/RoboKind, Cyberdyne, Diligent Robotics, Ekso Bionics, Kinova Robotics, ReWalk Robotics, Wandercraft, 1X Technologies, Apptronik, PAL Robotics, Sanctuary AI) is a **false positive**.

**Root cause:** The assessor agent was using simple-mean reconstruction `((mean - 1) / 4) � 100` and comparing against the published composite. The canonical formula in `site/scripts/lib/scoring.mjs::computeCompositeFromDimensions` includes an `integrationPremium = 10 � consistencyMult � weaknessFactor` term that adds up to +10 points for high-consistency entities with no weak dimensions. For Open Bionics (all dimensions 4.5/5, stdDev 0, weakDims 0): baseComposite 87.5 + integrationPremium 10.0 = published 97.5 ?.

**Validation:** `node site/scripts/validate-indexes.mjs` (which uses the canonical formula) emits ZERO formula warnings for any robotics-labs entity.

**Remediation:**
1. `.claude/agents/benchmark-research.md` � Composite Score section rewritten with full formula, integration premium, worked example, and reconstruction pseudocode.
2. `.claude/agents/overnight-assessor.md` � Added explicit math-hygiene flag rule: only flag if canonical reconstruct disagrees by >0.5pt. Simple-mean disagreements of 8�10pt for high-consistency entities are expected and must NOT be flagged.
3. Future cycle outputs should stop reproducing the math-hygiene flag for these entities.

**Carry-forward:** None. The flag is closed.

2. If substantive renewal confirmed: same note plus assessment of mandate scope changes
3. If NO vote and mandate lapses: emergency human-review required; lapse represents unprecedented UN peacekeeping governance failure with direct civilian protection consequences

**Resolution selected:** Option 1 (Permanent-floor designation framework) implemented as a structured `floorDesignation` payload attached to each designated entity record. The payload contains `designated`, `designatedDate`, `evidenceWindow`, `rationale`, `primaryDrivers[]`, `evidenceSummary[]`, `methodologyVersion` � surfaced as a public &ldquo;call out why&rdquo; disclosure on every entity page banner, the daily briefing &ldquo;Floor designations&rdquo; panel, and a new `/methodology#floor-designation` section. Composite resolves at zero by formula (all 8 dimensions at 1.0); designation is the formal methodology basis. Reversible when documented behavioral change is evidenced; same human-approval gate as any score change.

**Implementation:** `site/scripts/apply-floor-designation.mjs` (atomic, deterministic), `EntityDetail.tsx` banner, `DailyBriefing.tsx` `<FloorDesignationsPanel>` section, `methodology/page.tsx` `#floor-designation` section. Build verified: 1,201 pages prerender; all 5 designated entity pages render the disclosure.

**Re-rank impact:** Countries: 12 entities at composite 0 (was 11); ranks 173&ndash;184 shift up by 1 to fill the gap; Israel slots into rank 185 alphabetically (between Eritrea and Myanmar). AI Labs: ranks 49&ndash;50 retained (Palantir &lt; xAI alphabetically).

### New Methodology -- v1.2 (2026-05-11)

Name: Day-3 Sustained-Conduct Dimensional-Credit-Under-Sub-Threshold-Composite Rule

Rule: When sustained good-faith conduct over a defined observable window produces measurable upward dimensional pressure that reconstructs to a composite delta below the 5.0pt materiality threshold, the dimensional credit is carried forward as documented dimensional pressure rather than applied as a material composite upgrade.

First trigger: Ukraine (+3.1 sub-threshold) and Waymo (+3.2 sub-threshold). Status: on record; applies all future cycles.

### New Conduct Category -- external-accountability-reversal

FIRST POSITIVE-CONDUCT CATEGORY IN FRAMEWORK HISTORY. Applied to Hungary for ICC arrest-warrant enforcement reversal. All prior new categories documented harmful conduct. Definition: institution actively reverses prior non-compliance posture toward established external accountability mechanism. Three criteria: prior documented non-compliance, enacted reversal (not stated intent), practical effect on mechanism reach. Pairing rule: ICC-obligated country generates secondary INT credit; ICC mechanism generates collateral evidence in floor records of ICC-warranted entities. First applied 2026-05-13.

## 2026-05-21 -- WIDE CYCLE: 5 Formal Score Changes | 4 Band Crossings Proposed | 11 Sub-Threshold | 21 First-Baselines | 6 Floor Confirmations | 1 Human-Review Carry-Forward

> BAND-CROSSING-PROPOSED (4): Marshall Islands (upward, Developing to Functional), Timor-Leste (upward, Developing to Functional), Pakistan (downward, Developing to Critical), Anthropic (held, Functional/Established boundary, cycle 2).

### Summary -- 2026-05-21

The benchmark's widest single cycle: 49 entities assessed, 5 formal score changes (both directions for the first time), 4 band crossings proposed, 21 first-baselines established. Hungary's +6.3 is the first formal upgrade in benchmark history -- the canonical positive-evidence test case for the symmetric-evaluation rule. Mongolia +6.3 follows with UN-validated enacted legislation. The US -5.3 downgrade is triggered by the UNGA ICJ Climate vote (against, one of 8) plus ongoing immigration enforcement documentation. Croatia -7.8 is the cycle's largest downgrade, driven by Liberties.eu "Dismantler" classification. India -5.1 from Rohingya non-refoulement forced-sea event. The UNGA vote generated the widest single-event scoring footprint in benchmark history: 5 co-sponsor nations upward, 8 voting-against nations under negative pressure. xAI's first-baseline at 11.7 Critical makes it the AI Labs index's clearest governance failure entity, 48.3 points below Anthropic in the same index.

---

### HIGH PRIORITY -- Formal Score Changes (5 proposals; 4 APPLIED 2026-05-21; 1 HELD)

| Entity | Index | Published | Applied | Delta | Confidence | Band Change | Date | File |

| ~~**Mongolia**~~ | countries | 48.4 | **54.7** | **+6.3** | High | No (Functional sustained) | 2026-05-21 | [proposal](change-proposals/mongolia-2026-05-21.json) | **[APPLIED 2026-05-21]**
| **United States** | countries | 54.5 | **49.2** | **-5.3** | High | No (Functional sustained; below 50.0 for first time) | 2026-05-21 | [proposal](change-proposals/united-states-2026-05-21.json) |
| ~~**Croatia**~~ | countries | 48.4 | **40.6** | **-7.8** | Medium | No (Functional sustained; floor-proximate) | 2026-05-21 | [proposal](change-proposals/croatia-2026-05-21.json) | **[APPLIED 2026-05-21]**
| ~~**India**~~ | countries | 27.8 | **22.7** | **-5.1** | High | No (Developing sustained; 2.7pt above Critical) | 2026-05-21 | [proposal](change-proposals/india-2026-05-21.json) | **[APPLIED 2026-05-21]**

**Hungary (+6.3 UPGRADE -- FIRST IN BENCHMARK HISTORY):** Magyar government in office May 9 with two-thirds majority; 27 EU supermilestones committed; EPPO accession, PM term limits, Sovereignty Protection Office abolition in legislative pipeline. Conservative anchoring: reforms announced not enacted. INT and EQU lead the movement. May 27 EU funds reform plan and May 31 Sulyok compliance are forward milestones. Hungary math-hygiene drift (+1.57pt, 2 cycles) resolved in the upgrade calculation -- new dimensional scores produce 47.7 cleanly. Symmetric-evaluation rule canonical test case: PASSED.

**Mongolia (+6.3 UPGRADE):** HRDs Law enacted -- Northeast Asia's first. UN High Commissioner for Human Rights Turk public commendation. Active UN SOGI Expert visit May 18-29. Coherent rights leadership sustained under Russia/China geographic pressure. INT and ACC lead the movement. UN SOGI Expert conclusions pending (late May).

**United States (-5.3 DOWNGRADE):** UNGA ICJ Climate vote AGAINST (one of 8, joining Russia/Iran/Saudi Arabia cluster); pre-vote State Department cable opposing adoption documented. Immigration enforcement: 605,000+ deportations, 167,000+ ICE arrests; courts ruled third-country deportations unlawful; SIJS youth deferred action ended May 10. INT and EQU dimensions take largest cuts (-9.3 each). First crossing below 50.0 midpoint.

**Croatia (-7.8 DOWNGRADE -- LARGEST SINGLE-CYCLE OF CURRENT BATCH):** Liberties.eu 2026 "Dismantler" classification (EU's most serious rule-of-law tier; grouped with Bulgaria, Italy, Slovakia). Multi-area deterioration: judicial independence, press freedom, ACC structural failures. All 8 dimensions decline; EQU and ACC largest cuts (-9.4 each). At 40.6, Croatia is 0.6pt above the Functional/Developing boundary.

**India (-5.1 DOWNGRADE):** Indian Navy forced 40 Rohingya refugees (including children and elderly) into sea near Myanmar coast May 6-8. Non-refoulement violation; UN special investigator deployed; UNHRC condemnation. ACT and EQU take largest cuts (-6.2 each). IWT non-compliance (third carry-forward cycle). At 22.7, India is 2.7pt above Developing/Critical boundary -- boundary watch elevated.

**Marshall Islands:** UNGA A/80/L.65 adopted 141-8-28 -- Marshall Islands core co-sponsor; co-sponsorship maintained despite US Compact of Free Association dependency. 30-year climate advocacy now operationalized via binding-obligation legal architecture. INT and SYS dimensions lead uplift. At 41.4, 1.4pt above Functional floor.

**Timor-Leste:** ASEAN accession governance translation; Myanmar universal-jurisdiction prosecution arc maintained; clean rights record. Narrowest upward crossing distance of the cycle (0.6pt above floor). Confidence medium -- ASEAN accession not yet operationalized at the same intensity as Marshall Islands UNGA co-sponsorship.

**Pakistan (DOWNWARD -- requires special human review protocol):** 146,000+ Afghan refugee forcible returns in 2026 (HRW surge documentation); online speech amendments triggering journalist/activist detentions; UN HCHR Turk warning. Delta of -2.4 is sub-threshold alone but band-crossing protocol applies regardless of delta size. At 20.3, 0.3pt inside Critical -- most proximate boundary position in countries index. A single positive event could reverse the crossing.

**Anthropic (HELD -- Cycle 2):** DC Circuit "spectacular overreach" panel language on permanent record; no ruling yet issued; xAI CSAM failure sharpens sector contrast but does not move Anthropic's absolute score. Cycle-3 hold protocol should be established if ruling does not arrive before next wide cycle.

### Methodology v1.3 --- New Rulings (2026-05-22)

1. **Dismantler classification magnitude scales with starting position** -- identical Tier-1 institutional findings produce proportionately smaller movements at lower baselines where the concern is already partially priced in.
2. **Harm-enabled-then-accountability-applied dual-signal weighting** -- both harm-enabling record and accountability response are scored simultaneously at dimension level; net composite depends on relative severity of each signal.
3. **Reforms-contested-not-abandoned** -- sub-pattern within reforms-announced-not-enacted anchoring; distinguishes domain-specific negotiation (peripheral to upgrade driver) from programmatic abandonment (rebuts upgrade).

### Methodology v1.4 - New Rulings (2026-05-23)

1. **JUDICIAL-REMOVAL-OF-OPPOSITION-PARTY-LEADERSHIP** - new category established. Judicial removal of an opposition party governing structure is qualitatively distinct from individual arrests or press restrictions. Convention: -4 to -6 delta when (i) judicial action institutionally final, (ii) government does not restore status quo ante, (iii) downstream criminal enforcement follows. First application: Turkey 2026-05-23. Future-risk entities: Tunisia, Venezuela, El Salvador.

2. **FORWARD-TRIGGER-RESOLUTION-CONFIRMED-FIRED** - sub-threshold promotion protocol. When a scanner-documented forward trigger fires within the same cycle, promote the accumulator and add +1.5 to +2.5 uplift (+2.0 Tier-1 multilateral, +1.0 Tier-2 single-state). First application: Vanuatu 2026-05-23. Next candidate: Hungary May 27 Brussels signing.

3. **Confirming-Event Uplift for Sub-Threshold Accumulator Promotion** - when a second independent external source documents the same pattern materializing in a new incident, the confirming-event premium may cross the formal-apply threshold. First application: Amazon 2026-05-23.

## Special-Briefing Methodology Questions

> Source: `research/special-briefings/floor-and-critical-2026-06-11.md` (Special Briefing — "The Floor and the Critical Band"). These are interpretive questions raised by structural analysis of the bottom of the scale. **Flagged for human review — NOT auto-applied. No scores are changed by this briefing.**

### SBQ-1 (2026-06-11) — Should there be a corporate floor? [HUMAN REVIEW]
Corporations are currently exempted from the 0.0 floor by the all-anchor-collapse *formula mechanic*, not by an explicit judgment. The largest index (Fortune 500, 448 entities) has 52 Critical entities but zero at the floor; the lowest is GEO Group at 6.6 (private prisons, uniform `1.5×8`). Under the same "no remediation surface" logic that floors Ghost Robotics (weaponized product) and Palantir AI (military-contract product), are private-prison operators or weaponized-product corporations floor-*eligible*? The corporate ruling sub-taxonomy has no active-perpetration analog. **Decision needed:** introduce a `CORPORATE-ACTIVE-PERPETRATION-FLOOR` ruling with an explicit remediation-surface test, OR state explicitly why corporations are judged on a different bottom-of-scale logic — but do not leave the formula to make the call silently. (Most defensible external critique of the current record.)

### SBQ-2 (2026-06-11) — Is one 0–100 scale right for cross-type bottom-band comparison? [HUMAN REVIEW]
UnitedHealth (10.2) and Turkey (10.3) are within 0.1pt but fail in incommensurable ways: Turkey = governance collapse (BND/ACC/INT) across an ~85M-person state; UnitedHealth = stakeholder-harm collapse (ACC/EMP/EQU) within a bounded commercial relationship. Severity is within-type defensible, cross-type unsupported. **Decision needed:** add a per-type interpretive frame to Critical-band publication; suppress cross-type "league table" framing for the bottom band specifically; decide whether to publish any single global bottom ranking at all.

### SBQ-3 (2026-06-11) — Formalize the city→country floor-inheritance rule. [HUMAN REVIEW]
Five floor cities are capitals of floor states (coherent). But Bangui (parent CAR, 4.7) and Port-au-Prince (parent Haiti, 4.7) are at the 0.0 floor while their parent countries are not. Defensible on facts (non-state-actor collapse concentrated in the capital) but rests on case-by-case judgment. **Decision needed:** adopt an explicit `ATTRIBUTION-NON-STATE-ACTOR-AT-FLOOR-for-cities` rule so the asymmetry is rule-bound.

### SBQ-4 (2026-06-11) — Pre-register the cap→floor adjudication trigger. [HUMAN REVIEW]
The complicity-by-proxy cap (UAE 18.4, capped above floor because external sponsor + ICJ case unadjudicated) implies a path to the floor if the relevant ICJ case is adjudicated. **Decision needed:** pre-register that adjudication trigger so the cap/floor boundary is demonstrably rule-bound, not ad hoc.

### SBQ-5 (2026-06-11) — Flag F500 quantization clusters for first-baseline re-assessment. [HUMAN REVIEW / DATA QUALITY]
41 of the 52 F500 Critical entities sit at exactly 12.5 (16), 14.1 (12), or 18.8 (13) — uniform-anchor profiles consistent with placeholder baselines rather than measured assessment. **Action needed:** flag for first-baseline re-assessment. Data-quality question, not interpretive.

> Source: `research/special-briefings/exemplars-2026-06-11.md` (Special Briefing — "What Good Looks Like"). These are the symmetric top-of-scale counterparts to SBQ-1/SBQ-2, raised by structural analysis of the 64 Exemplary entities (composite ≥ 80). **Flagged for human review — NOT auto-applied. No scores are changed by this briefing.**

### SBQ-6 (2026-06-11) — Is "Exemplary" cross-type comparable, and should the top band carry a per-type interpretive frame? [HUMAN REVIEW]
The symmetric counterpart to SBQ-2 at the top of the scale. Open Bionics (97.5, a single assistive-prosthetics product line) and Switzerland (97.5, a whole-of-state assessment of ~8.8M people) share a band and an identical number on incommensurable evidentiary surfaces. Excellence is within-type defensible, cross-type unsupported. **Decision needed:** publish Exemplary-band placement with an explicit per-type interpretive frame; avoid a single cross-type "most compassionate institution" league table; decide whether any global top ranking is published at all.

### SBQ-7 (2026-06-11) — Do narrow-mandate entities reach Exemplary "by product category" the way corporations are exempted from the floor "by formula"? [HUMAN REVIEW]
The exact symmetric question to SBQ-1. Robotics labs are 26.0% Exemplary (13/50) — far above any other index (Fortune 500 is 1.8%) — because a single intrinsically pro-social product (assistive prosthetics/mobility: Open Bionics, Ottobock, Ekso, ReWalk, Wandercraft, Cyberdyne) satisfies the band on a narrow surface, with no requirement analogous to a sovereign's whole-of-population test. **Decision needed:** state explicitly that single-product entities are judged on a different top-of-scale logic (and why), OR introduce a breadth-of-mandate qualifier — but do not let narrowness of surface silently substitute for breadth of demonstrated compassion.

### SBQ-8 (2026-06-11) — Pre-register the equity gate as an explicit Exemplary criterion. [HUMAN REVIEW]
Equity (EQU) is the weakest dimension for 62 of the 64 exemplars, scores below 4.0 in 39 of them, and is the *only* sub-4.0 dimension in 37. The band is in practice an "everything-high-except-equity" band; the integration premium's `weaknessFactor` means a single sub-4.0 equity score is the entire distance between the band leaders (97.5) and its floor (~81). **Decision needed:** should reaching Exemplary require a minimum EQU floor (e.g. EQU ≥ 4.0), making the implicit pattern an explicit rule, so the band cannot be entered on a strong-everywhere-but-fairness profile?

### SBQ-9 (2026-06-11) — Flag low-Exemplary quantization clusters for first-baseline re-assessment. [HUMAN REVIEW / DATA QUALITY]
The top-of-scale symmetric counterpart to SBQ-5. Six robotics labs sit at exactly 83.0 and four entities (3 AI labs + Burlington) at exactly 81.4 — uniform near-anchor profiles consistent with placeholder first baselines rather than independently measured assessment. **Action needed:** flag for first-baseline re-assessment. Data-quality question, not interpretive.

### SBQ-10 (2026-06-11) — Pre-register the trajectory→band and compelled-vs-self-initiated rules for the top of the scale. [HUMAN REVIEW]
The record already withholds a top score from positive-but-insufficient movement — Hungary's six-cycle recovery (28.1 → 50.2) reaches only Functional, and Microsoft's compelled human-rights remedy is held sub-threshold in Established (65.3) under COMPELLED-REMEDY-NOT-SELF-CORRECTION. **Decision needed:** state explicitly, as published rules, that (a) Exemplary is conferred only on sustained self-initiated conduct, never on trajectory or compelled remedy, and (b) the compelled-remedy ceiling applies symmetrically at the top of the scale with its conversion trigger pre-registered — protecting Exemplary from being gamed by announcement or forced settlement.

> Source: `research/special-briefings/layoffs-despite-profits-2026-06-15.md` (Special Briefing — "Layoffs Despite Profits — The Corporate Boundaries Failure"). These are interpretive questions raised by analysis of the H1-2026 Fortune 500 restructuring wave and its two applied band crossings (P&G, Oracle). **Flagged for human review — NOT auto-applied. No scores are changed by this briefing.**

### SBQ-11 (2026-06-15) — P&G primary-source freshness/provenance question (FOUNDER-FLAGGED). [HUMAN REVIEW / DATA PROVENANCE]
The P&G downgrade (86.1 → 79.0, Exemplary → Established) is applied and the conduct is real, but its *primary* announcement article — `cnbc.com/2025/06/05/procter-gamble-job-cuts-restructuring.html` — is dated **June 2025**, roughly a year outside the standard 14-day freshness window. The corroborating NBC (rcna211263) and AOL articles carry the same 7,000 figure and "despite increasing profits" framing; the assessment dates the announcement "June 5, 2026." The founder flagged this in the 2026-06-13 scan context. **Open question:** is the June 5 *2026* announcement date independently verified, or did a stale 2025 primary source seed an in-window framing? **Action needed:** confirm the 2026 event against a clean in-window primary source, OR — if the underlying event is the June 2025 restructuring — re-examine whether it should have driven a 2026 in-window crossing at all. Do NOT re-score on this briefing's authority; resolve the date first. (Not fabrication — the harm is documented; the freshness of the anchor was not clean.)

### SBQ-12 (2026-06-15) — Formalize the distress-vs-profit-protection test as a named ruling. [HUMAN REVIEW]
The P&G crossing rests on "cut while profitable, for margin not survival" — currently an assessor judgment, not a codified category. **Decision needed:** introduce an explicit `PROFIT-PERIOD-WORKFORCE-REDUCTION` ruling with a stated financial-condition test (trailing/projected profitability + stated non-distress driver) so future profit-period layoffs are decided against a registered standard rather than case-by-case.

### SBQ-13 (2026-06-15) — Define the scoring threshold inside COERCIVE-SEVERANCE-STRUCTURE. [HUMAN REVIEW]
Oracle is the first application, but the category bundles distinct sub-harms: sign-or-forfeit consent, WARN-pay-absorbed-into-severance, unvested-share forfeiture, declined-parity. **Decision needed:** specify which sub-elements are *individually* scorable versus which require the *totality*, so a future company doing only one (e.g., sign-or-forfeit alone) is assessed predictably. The June 12 digest treats coercive consent as the primary element; make that primacy explicit in the ruling text.

### SBQ-14 (2026-06-15) — Severance generosity as an explicit Boundaries-positive offset. [HUMAN REVIEW]
Meta's sector-leading severance was credited with *preventing* a larger downgrade; Oracle's minimized severance *deepened* one. The offset currently operates implicitly. **Decision needed:** state whether — and how much — documented above-market transition support (severance weeks, health continuation, outplacement) can offset a profit-period or structured-layoff downgrade, so the Meta/Oracle asymmetry is rule-bound.

### SBQ-15 (2026-06-15) — Pre-register the cusp-conversion trigger for the corporate boundary cluster. [HUMAN REVIEW]
3M (20.3) and Cigna (20.3) sit where Oracle sat pre-crossing — fractions above the Critical line. **Decision needed:** pre-register that an Oracle-type structured-layoff event at either entity is a Developing → Critical conversion trigger, so the next crossing in this theme is demonstrably rule-bound rather than reactive.

> Source: `research/special-briefings/ai-governance-2026-06-15.md` (Special Briefing — "AI Governance Under Pressure"). These are raised by the conduct-vs-coercion, pre-adjudication, and worker-voice analysis of the AI Labs cohort under external pressure. **Flagged for human review — NOT auto-applied. No scores are changed by this briefing.**

### SBQ-16 (2026-06-15) — Pre-register the conduct-vs-coercion rule for compelled shutdowns/restrictions. [HUMAN REVIEW]
The Anthropic Fable 5 / Mythos 5 case establishes by precedent that a government-compelled model shutdown is scored on the entity's *conduct in the event* (transparency, apology, compliance) — net-neutral-to-mildly-positive — not as self-inflicted harm. Anthropic held at 59.1 (one sub-threshold −0.3 day) with ACC nudged 3.5→3.6. The rule is currently applied case-by-case in the assessment narrative, not as a published ruling. **Decision needed:** publish a COMPELLED-RESTRICTION-SCORED-ON-CONDUCT ruling with the conduct sub-criteria (disclosure, harm-acknowledgment, restoration effort) stated, symmetric to the COMPELLED-REMEDY-NOT-SELF-CORRECTION ceiling already used for Microsoft — so "compelled" is rule-bound at both the positive and negative ends.

### SBQ-17 (2026-06-15) — Pre-register the subpoena→enforcement adjudication trigger for AI labs. [HUMAN REVIEW]
The OpenAI 42-state AG subpoena is held sub-threshold under ALLEGATION-NOT-ADJUDICATED, with downward ACC/AWR pressure (conservative reconstruction 25.9, delta −1.6 < 5) leaving the composite at 27.5. The conversion conditions (enforcement action, settlement, adjudicated finding) appear in the assessment watch but not in a published ruling. **Decision needed:** pre-register the trigger that converts a multi-state AG investigation into a scorable ACC/INT downgrade, mirroring the FILED-BUT-UNADJUDICATED discipline used for Fortune-500 enforcement — so the discount's endpoint is demonstrably rule-bound, not ad hoc.

### SBQ-18 (2026-06-15) — Decide whether worker-voice is a scorable accountability signal or only a forward indicator. [HUMAN REVIEW]
The DeepMind/Google union vote (reported 98% of ~300 London staff, over military AI / Project Nimbus) is currently treated as a forward indicator with no composite effect; DeepMind/Google holds at 56.9 (weakest dimensions ACC 3.0, INT 3.0, BND 3.2 — exactly those a military-AI revolt implicates). **Decision needed:** state explicitly whether a documented worker revolt over an entity's harmful end-use can move a score, on which dimension (ACC signal-amplification vs. INT values-conduct gap), and under what trigger (management refusal, retaliation, contract continuation despite the vote) — so worker-voice is neither silently ignored nor silently over-weighted.

### SBQ-19 (2026-06-15) — Reconcile the "AI lab" label across the model-builder vs. parent-corporation split. [HUMAN REVIEW]
Microsoft (65.3), DeepMind/Google (56.9), Alphabet/Google (40.0), Amazon AWS AI (35.9), Amazon (12.8), Meta AI (26.3), and Meta Platforms (7.8) are all "big-tech AI," scored as distinct entities across two indexes with a 57.5-point spread. When the same conduct (e.g., Project Nimbus) implicates both the model-builder and the parent, the attribution rule between them is not published. **Decision needed:** state how shared conduct is attributed across the ai-labs entry and the Fortune-500 parent, so one corporate group's AI conduct is treated explicitly rather than incidentally across indexes.

---

> Source: `research/special-briefings/equity-tax-2026-06-16.md` (Special Briefing — "The Equity Tax"). These are interpretive questions raised by structural analysis of the Equity (EQU) dimension across all 1,156 entities. **Flagged for human review — NOT auto-applied. No scores are changed by this briefing.** IDs SBQ-20..23 reserved for this briefing. SBQ-20/SBQ-21 deepen and operationalize the earlier SBQ-8.

### SBQ-20 (2026-06-16) — Is the universal equity gap a finding about the world or an artifact of the anchors? [HUMAN REVIEW]
Equity is the weakest or tied-weakest dimension for 1,046 of 1,156 entities (90.5%), the strictly-lowest for 592 (51.2%), and the lowest-mean dimension in 6 of 7 indexes (global EQU mean 2.21 vs ~2.45–2.69 for the other seven; a 0.38-pt deficit vs the other-seven average). Critically, that deficit is **uniform across the entire quality spectrum** — it holds for Switzerland (97.5) and Sudan (0.0) alike — which is evidence that at least part of it is built into how the EQU anchors are set (disaggregated outcome data + independent audit + co-design, artifacts almost no institution produces) rather than purely a measure of conduct. **Decision needed:** is the EQU anchor ladder (`dimensions.ts` EQ1–EQ5) calibrated to the same realism as the other seven dimensions, or set to an aspirational standard that mechanically depresses the dimension everywhere? If aspirational-by-design, state it explicitly; if not, consider recalibrating the mid-rungs.

### SBQ-21 (2026-06-16) — Pre-register the equity gate as an explicit Exemplary criterion (operationalizes SBQ-8). [HUMAN REVIEW]
Of the 63 entities at composite ≥ 80, 61 have Equity as their weakest dimension and 36 carry EQU as their single sub-4.0 score; only Open Bionics (97.5, EQU 4.5) and Switzerland (97.5, EQU 4.0) clear it. The integration premium's `weaknessFactor` already makes one sub-4.0 EQU the difference between ~81.4 and 97.5 (worked example: Aflac 92.4 vs counterfactual 97.5 = 5.1pt from a single EQU notch). The band is in practice "high-everywhere-except-fairness." **Decision needed:** should reaching Exemplary require a minimum EQU floor (e.g. EQU ≥ 4.0), making the implicit pattern an explicit, published rule, so the band cannot be entered on a strong-everywhere-but-fairness profile?

### SBQ-22 (2026-06-16) — Should the weaknessFactor weight Equity distinctly, or remain symmetric? [HUMAN REVIEW]
`weaknessFactor = max(0, 1 − weakDims × 0.2)` (`site/src/lib/scoring.ts`) penalizes any dimension below 4.0 by a flat 0.2, dimension-agnostic. Because EQU is the near-universal weak point (§2/§4), in aggregate the integration premium is mostly an equity penalty in disguise — the consistency bonus is, field-wide, dominated by the single dimension institutions most often fail to clear. **Decision needed:** confirm that symmetric, dimension-agnostic treatment is intended, or decide whether equity warrants explicit separate treatment in the premium rather than being its silent dominant term.

### SBQ-23 (2026-06-16) — Surface each entity's weakest dimension (and the field-wide equity pattern) on the public surface. [HUMAN REVIEW / PRESENTATION]
The single most robust cross-index pattern in the record — EQU is the weakest dimension for 9 of 10 entities — is currently invisible at the entity-page level, where a reader sees a composite and a band but not "this entity's floor is fairness, like almost everyone's." **Decision needed:** whether to surface each entity's weakest dimension and the field-wide equity pattern as a reader-facing signal (e.g., on EntityDetail), as the clearest single statement of what the benchmark measures. Transparency/presentation question, not a scoring change.

> Source: `research/special-briefings/state-of-institutional-compassion-2026.md` (Flagship Annual — "The State of Institutional Compassion — 2026"). These are field-level methodology questions raised by the inaugural flagship synthesis across all 1,156 entities and 7 indexes. **Flagged for human review — NOT auto-applied. No scores are changed by this report.** IDs SBQ-24..26 reserved for this report; the individual briefings' own flags (corporate floor, cross-type bottom-band framing, city-inheritance rule, cap→floor trigger, equity anchors) remain live under their existing IDs and are not re-filed here.

### SBQ-24 (2026-06-16) — Should the flagship publish a single cross-index "state of the field" distribution as one number, given bands are not cross-type comparable? [HUMAN REVIEW / PRESENTATION]

The flagship presents the unified five-band distribution (Critical 177 / Developing 535 / Functional 248 / Established 133 / Exemplary 63) as one field. This is defensible descriptively — it is what the record contains — but it invites a cross-type read the framework cannot support (a robotics lab in Exemplary and a sovereign in Exemplary are not "equally good"; severity and excellence are calibrated within-type). Decision needed: publish the unified distribution with a standing prominent per-type interpretive caveat, or publish only per-index distributions and reserve the unified count for internal use. Report recommendation: the former, with the caveat made prominent. (Generalizes the within-type-only comparability flags raised by the Floor-and-Critical and Exemplars briefings.)

### SBQ-25 (2026-06-16) — Is the near-universal Equity gap (90.5%) a finding about the world or an artifact of the Equity bar? [HUMAN REVIEW / CALIBRATION]

Equity is the weakest or tied-weakest dimension for 1,046/1,156 entities (90.5%) and the strictly-lowest for 593 (51.3%), with a global mean of 2.21 — the lowest of all eight dimensions, holding across the entire quality spectrum (Switzerland 97.5 to Sudan 0.0). Because the gap holds even for institutions that clear high bars on the other seven dimensions, it is at least partly a real conduct finding. But the Equity top-anchors (disaggregated outcome data, independent audits, community co-design) are demanding enough that some universality may be anchor-calibration rather than conduct. Decision needed: commission a calibration review of the Equity anchors against the other seven before the flagship leans on the equity gap as its signature finding in future editions. (Deepens SBQ-20 from the Equity Tax briefing to flagship scope.)

### SBQ-26 (2026-06-16) — How should the flagship represent within-2026 movement without implying a multi-year trend the data cannot support? [HUMAN REVIEW / EDITORIAL POLICY]

The inaugural edition reports the ~20 applied cycles since 2026-04-15 explicitly as a single-season "scoring season," not a multi-year trend — the benchmark's structured data is 2026 only. As future years accumulate, a standing rule is needed for when directional language ("the field is declining") becomes warranted, and how the 2026 distribution is treated as the trend baseline. Decision needed: (a) define the minimum number of annual cycles before the flagship may make trend (vs. snapshot) claims, and (b) pre-register the 2026 five-band distribution and field median (35.9) as the official baseline anchor.

> Source: `research/special-briefings/famine-as-a-scored-event-2026-06-25.md` (Special Briefing — "Famine as a Scored Event"). Raised by analysis of the June 2026 multi-theatre famine cluster (Sudan 0.0, Nigeria 18.0, Somalia 4.7). **Flagged for human review — NOT auto-applied. No scores are changed by this briefing.** ID SBQ-27 reserved for this briefing.

### SBQ-27 (2026-06-25) — Formalize a famine-attribution weighting schema for IPC Phase 5 triggers. [HUMAN REVIEW / CALIBRATION]
The famine cohort shows an identical-category adjudicated-equivalent trigger (IPC Phase 5 famine declared/projected) correctly weighted differently by causation: Sudan (RSF-siege **perpetration** → reinforces the 0.0 floor), Nigeria (state **prevention-failure** → −3.9, Developing→Critical band crossing applied 2026-06-19), Somalia (drought-led **natural-disaster-overlay**, state cooperating with UN/WFP → no move, near-floor 4.7 held). Each outcome is individually defensible and reconciles with the canonical formula, but the *weighting* of the three causation classes is applied case-by-case by the assessor, not by a published rule — a reader cannot reconstruct from a written schema why Nigeria’s prevention-failure famine was scored −3.9 rather than −6, or why Somalia’s larger projected caseload moved nothing. **Decision needed:** introduce a named `FAMINE-ATTRIBUTION-WEIGHTING` ruling distinguishing perpetration vs prevention-failure vs natural-disaster-overlay, each with a stated magnitude band and a pre-registered conversion trigger (e.g., a formal IPC Phase 5 declaration with documented state-response failure for Somalia’s Buur Hakaba window, ~2026-06-30). This connects to the open Sahel calibration question (Mali 12.5 vs Burkina Faso 6.3) and the existing ACTIVE-STATE-PERPETRATION reweight. Do NOT re-score on this briefing’s authority; the question is whether to codify the standard, not to change any number.

## 2026-06-18 -- 1 Change Proposal | HHS OIG Medicare Advantage Denial-Rate Trigger (Humana) | 19 Confirmations

### Summary -- 2026-06-18

One scored change proposal generated this cycle: Humana (51.6 -> 40.6, -11.0, fortune-500, WITHIN-BAND DOWNGRADE, Functional sustained, medium confidence). Trigger: new HHS OIG report (surfaced June 12-15 2026) finding Humana denied 72% of LTCH and 54% of IRF Medicare Advantage admission requests -- far above the ~42% peer average of 16 smaller MA organizations -- with ~95% of appealed skilled-nursing denials overturned across the three largest MA insurers, indicating most initial denials were not clinically warranted. This is a Tier-5 federal watchdog finding bearing directly on ACT (action calibrated to need), EQU (priority for vulnerable post-acute patients), EMP (validation of harmed patients), ACC/INT (ownership of the pattern), and SYS (structural denial model). Partial mitigant: Humana publicly committed to reduce Medicare Advantage prior authorizations in 2026 -- a documented but unproven correction signal that keeps ACC off the floor. No band change; Humana stays in the Functional band at its lower boundary. 19 other entities confirm at delta 0.0, including a high-severity Critical-band cluster (Russia 0.0, Israel 0.0, Iran 2.5, DRC 2.3, Bolivia 6.3, Burkina Faso 6.3, Mali 12.5, India 15.6) and Ford Motor (UAW Kentucky Truck Plant strike AVERTED via tentative agreement -- resolved notice is a process event, not scorable harm). Scanner correction: DRC carried 20.3; live index authoritative at 2.3 (corrected).

### Standard -- 2026-06-18 (Within-Band Downgrade, NEW TONIGHT)

| Entity | Index | Published | Proposed | Delta | Confidence | Band Change | Date | File |
|--------|-------|-----------|----------|-------|------------|-------------|------|------|
| **Humana** | fortune-500 | 51.6 | **40.6** | **-11.0** | Medium | No (Functional -> Functional, lower boundary) | 2026-06-18 | [proposal](change-proposals/humana-2026-06-18.json) |

**Humana (TIER-5-FEDERAL-WATCHDOG-FINDING -- HHS OIG MEDICARE ADVANTAGE DENIAL RATES):** The published 51.6 predates the June 2026 HHS OIG report, which found Humana denied 72% of LTCH admission requests and 54% of IRF requests under Medicare Advantage -- far above the ~42% peer average. Across the three largest MA insurers, ~95% of appealed skilled-nursing denials were overturned, indicating most initial denials were not clinically warranted. Post-acute LTCH/IRF patients are among the highest-need, lowest-power Medicare Advantage beneficiaries (elderly, disabled, seriously ill), making the inverse-prioritization pattern an acute EQU and ACT failure. Dimension moves: ACT 3.5 -> 2.5 (largest; action calibrated to cost, not need), EQU 2.5 -> 2.0 (EQ2 Priority for Vulnerable: highest-need patients face highest denial rates), EMP 3.0 -> 2.5 (harm met with denial-first, reversed only on appeal), ACC 3.0 -> 2.5 and INT 3.0 -> 2.5 (deny-for-profit pattern contradicts stated member-care mission), SYS 3.5 -> 3.0 (prior-auth model is structural driver of denied care). AWR 3.0 and BND 3.0 unchanged. Partial mitigant: Humana 2026 PA-reduction pledge is a documented correction signal that keeps ACC off the floor. Stays within Functional band (40.6 is Functional lower boundary). Watch: CMS enforcement action or reversal of the 2026 PA-reduction commitment would warrant a further move toward the Developing band.

Confirmed cases rose to 1,307 with 377 deaths; approximately 15 million people across DRC's northeast are now affected; Uganda has 19 cases; no approved vaccine exists for this strain. DRC's near-floor 2.3 is reinforced but not lowered -- response weakness is already priced; the floor-crossing trigger is documented deliberate obstruction of WHO response corridors, which has not occurred. The spread to Haut-Uele, which borders South Sudan (0.0 floor, unrelated crises) and CAR, creates the June series first documented compounding cross-border epidemiological scenario.

Secondary lead: Israeli forces launched more than 100 airstrikes on Lebanon on June 30 -- the same day the ceasefire framework was renewed -- killing 83 and wounding 141. The harm is attributed to Israel (Israel's floor at 0.0 reinforced); Lebanon's 17.2 is unchanged on its own conduct. The same attribution principle applied on June 29 (Iran-Gulf) and June 30 (Israel-Lebanon) operated consistently in the same cycle, the first time two parallel attribution chains have resolved in a single assessment set.

Additional findings: Venezuela Day 6 -- toll rose to 1,719 dead / 46,600 missing; US doubled commitment to $300M; net sub-threshold both directions; July 8 window remains. ### Summary -- 2026-07-07

Two sub-threshold-but-real negative findings were documented with watch flags this cycle: Venezuela (STRONG downward -- canonical recompute 18.0 -> 15.3, delta -2.7, on documented earthquake-response failure: "the state has been the last responder" per WOLA; forensic-pathologist undercount allegation of "not even a third" of the true toll) and Cuba (downward -- canonical recompute 32.8 -> 29.7, delta -3.1, on a third islandwide blackout in six months). Two additional plain "downward" watch flags were logged: Pakistan (domestic crackdown -- mass preventive detention, 27-channel media ban, continued Afghan-refugee deportation) and China (Ethnic Unity Law now in force, reinforces existing Critical anchors, no discrete move).

The Mali (12.5) vs. Burkina Faso (6.3) cross-peer calibration flag -- routed to coordinator level 2026-06-24 -- reaches its **fourteenth consecutive day** unresolved. This cycle formally escalates the flag as a methodology-governance item requiring coordinator/meta-level review with a set timeline, rather than continuing as a routine nightly carry-forward note.

Four simultaneous priority-cluster swaps: Pakistan, Cuba, Afghanistan, and United States entered; South Sudan, Haiti, UnitedHealth Group, and Palestine dropped (no new in-window escalation for any of the four departures).

Scanner-level false-positive pre-screening debuts as a distinct metric this cycle: 5 signals screened before reaching the assessment queue (Apple -- dated Dec-2024 DRC litigation; Midjourney -- routine discovery-motion filing; GCC labor-rights batch -- dated evidence outside window; Meta/xAI/Grok -- forward-looking EU AI Act deadline, not a dated compliance action; Myanmar -- 100,000-fatality ACLED milestone scored moderate (20) rather than as a fresh major event (40), avoiding overweighting a cumulative-total crossing). This is a new, earlier-stage screening capability and is not directly comparable to the July 3-6 "15 FP screens" figure, which measured assessor-level dispositions of the 15 priority entities under the seven established categories (attribution/other-state, non-state, exogenous, pre-adjudication, double-count, floor-limitation, duplicate-control). Fourteen of tonight's 15 confirmations still rest on that same assessor-level framework; the United States required a new "net-mixed judicial-check" disposition not previously used.

## 2026-07-08 -- Zero Score Changes | Queue Clear (Third Consecutive Cycle) | Mali-Burkina Faso Calibration Flag SHARPENED BIDIRECTIONALLY (15 Days) | 0 Proposals | 15 Confirmations

### Summary -- 2026-07-08

Zero new score proposals. The pending queue remains empty for the **third consecutive cycle** (El Salvador applied 2026-07-05; queue entered 07-06, 07-07, and 07-08 all empty). Three rotation-state integrity corrections tonight -- the highest single-cycle count so far: Turkey composite drift corrected 15.1 -> 10.3; Pakistan rank corrected 154 -> 153; Kenya composite drift corrected 33.9 -> 35.9. All three now match the published index exactly.

Four simultaneous priority-cluster swaps: Turkey, Burkina Faso, Kenya, and xAI/Grok entered; Afghanistan, Iran, Lebanon, and United States dropped (no new in-window escalation for any of the four departures).

Ten of fifteen assessed entities (67%) carry a downward watch flag tonight -- the highest density recorded in the July series, more than double the four flags logged on 07-07 -- even as the proposal count stayed at zero. This is the anti-false-positive-gaming discipline functioning as designed: real, sub-threshold deterioration is documented transparently across most of the assessed set without being aggregated into a scoreable delta.

The Mali (12.5) vs. Burkina Faso (6.3) cross-peer calibration flag -- routed to coordinator level 2026-06-24 -- reaches its **fifteenth consecutive day** unresolved. Tonight is the first cycle where new evidence sharpens the flag from BOTH directions simultaneously: Burkina Faso's UN human-rights office was permanently closed (Jul 2), a discrete accountability-infrastructure removal that genuinely supports Burkina Faso's lower position. But the same evidence surfaces a second, previously latent question -- Mali's own 12.5 baseline is a uniform-1.5 seed that has never been individually re-derived against Mali's own atrocity findings (JNIM/FLA Bamako siege), unlike Burkina Faso's evidence-driven 6.3 reweight (2026-06-01). Both assessment files (Burkina Faso, Mali) independently recommend the coordinator treat this as TWO separate calibration findings rather than one closing adjustment.

xAI/Grok's floor (0.0) absorbs a new, more specific child-safety allegation: the deepfake-CSAM class action was amended (Jul 7) to add two anonymous minor plaintiffs with named-pattern detail (a photo of an 11-year-old used to generate ~7,000 sexually explicit images; a 14-year-old's graduation photo used similarly). The existing pending change proposal (on file since 2026-05-13) is reinforced, not superseded.

### Summary -- 2026-07-09

Zero new score proposals. The pending queue remains empty for the fourth consecutive cycle (El Salvador applied 2026-07-05; queue entered 07-06, 07-07, 07-08, and 07-09 all empty). Two rotation-state integrity corrections tonight: Uganda's rotation-state had drifted to 15.3/Critical/rank 141 with no corresponding entry in APPLIED_CHANGES.md (the same class of bug previously documented for El Salvador and Mali); corrected to the published 20.3/Developing/144. Myanmar's rotation-state rank had drifted to 191; corrected to the published 186 (composite and band already matched at 0/Critical).

Two special-attention boundary re-checks close out sub-threshold tonight. Anthropic (59.1, Functional, 0.9pt below Established) absorbed a genuine but singular transparency ding: a hidden Claude Code steganographic tracker (active since roughly March 2026, undisclosed, flagging users on Chinese IP/timezone endpoints) was discovered and confirmed by an Anthropic engineer as an unannounced anti-distillation experiment; Anthropic removed it around Jul 1. Maximum defensible move is -1.3 (INT 3.2 to 3.0, ACC 3.5 to 3.3), well under the 5-point threshold. Confirmed at 59.1, downward watch maintained. Conversion trigger: a second undisclosed telemetry episode, evidence the tracking was broader or retained after removal, or a regulator/court finding of deceptive practice. Meta Platforms required a published-baseline correction: the cycle directive described Meta as "published 60" at "the 60.0 Established/Functional boundary." Meta's actual published score is 7.8 (Critical), rank 446 of 447 in fortune-500.json -- verified against the live index, the Meta entity-record, and rotation-state, which all agree. The 1.4 trillion dollar youth-safety penalty demand disclosed this week is a litigation maximum-figure already priced into the 7.8, not new conduct. Confirmed at 7.8, downward watch maintained.

Two gravest-characterization findings sustain existing floors and cannot move them lower. Sudan (0.0): a UN inquiry concluded (Jul 9) that RSF mass killings and gang rapes amount to genocide -- the gravest international-law characterization the benchmark has recorded to date. Myanmar (0.0): the post-coup civil-war death toll passed 100,000 (ACLED, Jul 1), with the junta responsible for roughly 71% of civilian deaths. Both are floor-sustaining, not scoreable moves. Israel (0.0) and Yemen (0.0) round out four floor confirmations tonight on continuing own-conduct (settlement expansion; Houthi staff detention).

Disease continues to dominate the humanitarian layer without being scoreable against government conduct: DRC's Ebola toll hit 600 (fastest-growing outbreak on record, 1,759 cases), while Uganda reported a wholly separate Marburg outbreak (Jun 30) layered atop its already-active Ebola response; Uganda's prompt WHO notification is neutral-to-mildly-positive own-response conduct. Venezuela's earthquake reached day 16 (toll 3,899, up from 3,535); the evidenced response-failure move remains -2.7 for the third consecutive re-check, still sub-threshold. Downward watch continues on China (19.5), Pakistan (17.2), Nigeria (18.0), and Lebanon (17.2) -- all continuations of already-priced patterns.

Seven simultaneous priority-cluster swaps: Lebanon, Myanmar, Anthropic, Meta Platforms, Uganda, Yemen, and Haiti entered; Turkey, Ukraine, Cuba, Burkina Faso, Russia, Kenya, and xAI/Grok dropped (no new in-window escalation for any of the seven departures).

## 2026-07-10 -- One Change Proposal (Tunisia, First-Baseline, PENDING) | Israel Material Floor-Reinforcement | Mali-Burkina Faso Calibration Flag Seventeenth Day | 1 Proposal | 14 Confirmations

### Summary -- 2026-07-10

One new score proposal enters the pending queue tonight, breaking the four-consecutive-cycle empty-queue streak (Jul 6-9). Tunisia received its first individual assessment: the published 34.4 (rank 109, Developing) was a bulk-import placeholder with `last_assessed: null`, never individually checked. The evidence-derived composite is 23.8 (-10.6), remaining within the Developing band (no band crossing). The downgrade is driven by Accountability (2.5->1.6) and Equity (2.0->1.6), reflecting the July 8, 2026 sentencing of Sihem Bensedrine -- ex-president of Tunisia's own Truth and Dignity Commission -- to 25 years in prison, plus the collective expulsion of 12,000+ sub-Saharan migrants (Jan-Apr 2025) with documented torture, mass "conspiracy" trials up to 66 years, and the August 2025 shutdown of Tunisia's independent information-access authority. The proposed 23.8 sits above Critical-band peers Turkey (17.6) and China (19.5), which the assessor calls defensible given Tunisia's smaller scale of repression and larger remaining civil-liberties space (Freedom House 2026: Partly Free, 42/100). Confidence: medium. **This proposal carries `status: "proposed"` in `research/change-proposals/tunisia.json` and has NOT been applied. The live index composite for Tunisia remains 34.4 pending founder review.**

Two rotation-state integrity corrections tonight: Tunisia's rotation-state had drifted to 32.4/developing/rank111; corrected to match the published 34.4/developing/rank109 (placeholder drift, same bug class previously documented for El Salvador, Mali, Uganda, and Myanmar). Per the assessor-contract, rotation-state mirrors PUBLISHED scores only -- the proposed 23.8 lives exclusively in the change-proposal file. Somalia's rotation-state rank was corrected 187->179 (composite/band already matched at 4.7/critical).

Israel (0.0, floor) recorded a MATERIAL floor-reinforcing finding, distinguished from a routine floor-confirmation: Gaza territorial control expanded from roughly 53% to nearly 70% during the nominal ceasefire (NPR, Jul 10), described by Netanyahu as a deliberate "step-by-step plan," with 200+ Palestinians killed since the ceasefire began. Sudan (0.0) and Russia (0.0) round out floor confirmations: Sudan on the Jul 9-10 El Obeid siege warning following the Jul 9 UN genocide finding for El Fasher; Russia as perpetrator of the Jul 10 Kyiv/Korosten/Zaporizhzhia mass-casualty strikes. South Sudan (0.0) is confirmed on continuing famine-risk conditions with conflict-driven access blockage.

Disease and famine fronts continue in Central/East Africa without a new own-conduct step-change: DRC's Ebola toll reached 625/1,792 (up from 600), with suspected spread to Kisangani; Somalia's Burhakaba district surpassed the Phase-5 famine malnutrition threshold; both near-floor confirmed. Venezuela's earthquake toll (day 17) topped 3,800 -- essentially flat against day 16's 3,899, the first plateau this cycle -- with the evidenced response-failure move holding at approximately -2.7, sub-threshold for a fourth consecutive re-check. Haiti's US TPS work-authorization stopgap expired today (Jul 10, ~350k affected) -- US-attributable conduct, NOT Haiti's own conduct; Haiti confirmed near-floor at 4.7 on its own state collapse.

Yemen offers a rare positive-direction data point: the largest-ever UN/ICRC prisoner exchange reportedly began Jul 10. Yemen was not in tonight's assessed cluster; flagged as an upward-watch item for a future cycle.

The Mali (12.5) vs. Burkina Faso (6.3) cross-peer calibration flag -- routed to coordinator level 2026-06-24, escalated 2026-07-07, sharpened bidirectionally 2026-07-08, carried as standing coordinator/meta-level review 2026-07-09 -- reaches its **seventeenth consecutive day** tonight, with no resolution timeline set.

Five false positives were screened at the scanner level, including Anthropic (Claude ID facial-verification, Claude Code source leak, Abnormal AI trademark suit -- none meet the specified conversion trigger for Anthropic's boundary-watch status).

## 2026-07-11 -- Tunisia Reaffirmed (Day 2, STILL PENDING) | Bolivia New Entrant + NEW Calibration Flag | Mali-Burkina Faso Calibration Flag Eighteenth Day | Yemen Upward-Watch Retracted | 0 New Proposals | 14 Confirmations

### Summary -- 2026-07-11

Zero new change proposals. The one open proposal (Tunisia) is REAFFIRMED, not modified: new within-window evidence -- the UN Human Rights Council's 62nd session closing (Jul 8) with a deep-concern statement on Tunisia's civic-space crackdown, plus corroborating detail that the Bensedrine sentence carries a fine of roughly US $600 million alongside the 25-year prison term -- is fully consistent with the existing 23.8 basis. The figure is unchanged; no duplicate proposal was opened. **The proposal remains `status: "proposed"` and the published Tunisia composite stays at 34.4.** This is now day 2 of the open proposal.

Bolivia enters the priority cluster for the first time tonight. Blockade-related protest deaths have risen to at least 24 (up from 17), and police arrested Vicente Salazar, the leading figure of the Tupac Katari farmers' federation, in El Alto in early July; prosecutors are seeking his pretrial detention. This evidence is directionally negative, which forecloses an upgrade under anti-false-positive screening, but the documented harm is not atrocity-scale, so the outcome is a confirmation at 6.3 (unchanged). A NEW calibration flag is raised alongside the confirmation: Bolivia's 6.3 sits within 1.6 points of Burkina Faso (6.3) and Somalia (4.7), Critical-band peers facing qualitatively different conditions (armed insurgency, famine/state fragility) than an elected government under an austerity-driven economic crisis. This is recorded as flag-for-review, routed to coordinator/meta-level review -- NOT resolved unilaterally tonight.

Iran's political executions reached a multi-decade high (39+ since Feb 28; 12 more death sentences confirmed Jul 5; 6,500+ arrested since late Feb), but the near-floor arithmetic (2.5 points to the 0.0 floor) makes a >=5pt move impossible regardless of evidence severity; confirmed at 2.5 with a STRONG downward watch. Separately, the US-Iran ceasefire collapsed Jul 8 with the US striking ~80 targets inside Iran -- this harm is attributed to the United States' own-conduct record, not scored against Iran, and is logged here for cross-reference.

Yemen's largest-ever prisoner exchange (~1,750 detainees) -- logged in last night's (2026-07-10) digest as a rare upward-watch positive -- COLLAPSED on its scheduled Jul 10 start day (Houthi refusal to proceed; ICRC cancelled the staged Djibouti flights). Per integrity rules, a reversed positive is not carried forward: the 2026-07-10 upward-watch flag is explicitly RETRACTED tonight. Yemen's floor (0.0) is unaffected either way.

Four floor countries recorded materially reinforcing evidence tonight without any possibility of a numeric score change: Sudan (HRC-ordered urgent inquiry into the El Obeid siege, ~560k civilians trapped, following the earlier El Fasher genocide-markers finding), Israel (Gaza territorial control now ~70%, Gaza media office says 80%; 1,092+ Palestinians killed and 3,507+ wounded since the ceasefire began), Myanmar (Jul 11 junta airstrike killed 22 displaced people sheltering at a Sagaing monastery), and Afghanistan (8,466 Afghans expelled from Pakistan in three days; systematic gender persecution continues; rotation-state rank corrected 189->182).

Remaining Critical-band entities confirm without new discrete step-changes: Venezuela (18.0, STRONG downward watch, earthquake toll flat near 3,889-3,899 for a second night, evidenced move remains ~-2.7 sub-threshold for a fifth consecutive re-check), China (19.5, Ethnic Unity Law enforcement continues; a Tibetan activist's self-immolation death at UN HQ; a rare, non-structural positive -- Zion Church pastor Ezra Jin released to US custody after Trump-Xi intervention -- does not move the systemic-repression score), Pakistan (17.2, Operation Shaaban reports 88 militants killed in Balochistan since Jul 5), Nigeria (18.0, WFP/Cadre Harmonise Jul 2 report projects 35-36M food insecure, worst in a decade), Lebanon (17.2, fresh fatal Israeli strike Jul 6 killed 4, dominant harm remains external), Mali (12.5, renewed JNIM/FLA coordinated offensive Jul 4), and Burkina Faso (6.3, 22+ soldiers/militia killed in a weekend attack near Dedougou).

The Mali (12.5) vs. Burkina Faso (6.3) cross-peer calibration flag -- routed to coordinator level 2026-06-24 -- reaches its **eighteenth consecutive day** tonight, now running alongside the brand-new Bolivia calibration flag. Five false positives were screened at the scanner level, including a date-verification catch on El Salvador's re-election amendment (confirmed approved Jul 2025, not 2026, across three independent sources) and Anthropic's Claude Sonnet 5 release / consciousness-research announcements (disclosed product news, does not meet the conversion trigger).

## 2026-07-12 -- Tunisia Reaffirmed (Day 3, STILL PENDING) | Anthropic China-Backdoor Allegation Held (Conversion Trigger Not Met) | Mali-Burkina Faso Calibration ~19 Days | 0 New Proposals | 14 Confirmations

### Summary -- 2026-07-12

Zero new change proposals. The one open proposal (Tunisia) is REAFFIRMED for a third consecutive cycle: a Tunis court sentenced 21 opposition figures (Ennahda leaders, ex-officials, lawyers) to 12-35yr terms on Jul 8, with Rached Ghannouchi receiving a 14-year sentence in absentia. This is fully consistent with the existing 23.8 basis; the figure is unchanged and no duplicate proposal was opened. **The proposal remains `status: "proposed"` and the published Tunisia composite stays at 34.4.**

The headline governance story tonight is Anthropic. Between July 8-10, China's Ministry of Industry and Information Technology (MIIT) / National Vulnerability Database platform alleged that Claude Code contains an undisclosed "backdoor" transmitting user location/identity without consent. The assessor tested this rigorously against Anthropic's pre-defined conversion trigger ("a second undisclosed telemetry episode OR a regulator/court deceptive-practice finding") and found NEITHER prong met: (a) this is best read as a rival government's re-characterization of the already-priced March anti-distillation tracker, not a genuine second independently-corroborated episode -- Anthropic had already scheduled its removal for the Jul 2 release, before the Chinese alert; (b) an allegation by a geopolitically-motivated rival government's cybersecurity agency is not an adjudicated regulator or court finding. Anthropic's own-conduct residue (released versions did transmit location/identity signals without explicit consent) is real but modest, largely priced, and mitigated by the pre-scheduled removal. CONFIRM 59.1, with a HEIGHTENED downward watch (converts on an independently-verified recurrence or a neutral-regulator/court finding).

Venezuela's earthquake death toll climbed to 4,333 (from ~3,889), but a threshold re-check confirms the climb is predominantly continued body-recovery from collapsed buildings -- natural-disaster attribution, not new own-conduct failure. The cumulative evidenced own-conduct move deepens modestly (toward the low -3s) but stays sub-threshold. CONFIRM 18.0, strong downward watch sustained.

Two floor countries recorded materially reinforcing evidence without any possibility of a numeric move: Israel (5 more Palestinians killed Jul 12, post-ceasefire toll 1,098+ killed / 3,535 injured) and Yemen (the ~1,750-detainee prisoner exchange remains collapsed despite Jul 11 "renewed commitments"; the prior reversed positive is not carried).

Near-floor confirmations continue: DRC (2.3, Ebola toll 625 deaths / 1,792 cases, natural attribution), Iran (2.5, executions at a multi-decade high, own-conduct priced; US ceasefire-collapse strikes on Iran and IRGC retaliation against four Gulf states attributed to US conduct, not scored against Iran), and Ethiopia (4.7, most-stale Tier-1 record resolved -- sustained Ethiopia-Eritrea war-risk documented but no confirmed new dated clash this window).

Remaining Critical-band entities confirm without new discrete step-changes: China (19.5, Ethnic Unity Law and Hong Kong enforcement continue, fully priced), Pakistan (17.2, Operation Shaaban toll reaches 102 alleged militants as of Jul 12, security-source-reported and unverified), Nigeria (18.0, Jul 2 WFP/Cadre Harmonise record remains operative), Lebanon (17.2, fresh Jul 10 and Jul 12 Israeli strikes remain the dominant harm, not Lebanese own conduct), Mali (12.5, six-day JNIM/FLA battle at Anefis), and Burkina Faso (6.3, 22+ soldiers/militia killed near Dedougou). Uganda (20.3) confirmed with a neutral watch -- surveillance-driven containment of a Marburg case and 20 Ebola spillover cases is a genuine but non-structural operational positive.

The Mali (12.5) vs. Burkina Faso (6.3) cross-peer calibration flag -- routed to coordinator level 2026-06-24 -- reaches its **nineteenth consecutive day** tonight, still running alongside the Bolivia calibration flag (opened 2026-07-11, not assessed tonight). Six false positives were screened at the scanner level, including a date-verification catch on China (Dalai Lama 90th-birthday/monk-suicide references drawn from HRW's 2026 World Report, a 2025-period document) and confirmation that a viral Indonesia humanoid-robot "freak out" video was staged/choreographed.

Assessor rotation-state correction: Ethiopia rank corrected 175 to 176 (published-value alignment only; composite/band unchanged). No subdimension sidecars were written tonight (zero dimension changes across all 15 entities).

## 2026-07-13 -- Tunisia Reaffirmed (Day 4, STILL PENDING) | Iran Attribution Split (US Conduct Logged, Not Scored vs Iran) | Mali-Burkina Faso Calibration ~20 Days | 0 New Proposals | 14 Confirmations

### Summary -- 2026-07-13

Zero new change proposals. The one open proposal (Tunisia) is REAFFIRMED for a fourth consecutive cycle: no new dated escalation surfaced beyond the already-reflected Jul 8 mass sentencing (21 opposition figures, 12-35yr terms; Rached Ghannouchi 14yr in absentia; Sihem Bensedrine 25yr + heavy fine). A fresh HRW piece ("Tunisia: Harsh Sentences for Rights Defenders," published Jul 7) restates the same operative crackdown record rather than adding a new trigger. The figure (23.8) is unchanged; no duplicate proposal was opened. **The proposal remains `status: "proposed"` and the published Tunisia composite stays at 34.4** (verified directly against `site/src/data/indexes/countries.json`).

Iran (2.5) presented the cycle's cleanest attribution-split test: own-conduct executions/repression intensify at a multi-decade high, but near-floor arithmetic (2.5 points to the absolute floor) forecloses any >=5pt move regardless. Separately, the collapsing US-Iran ceasefire produced fresh US strikes on Iranian targets near the Strait of Hormuz on Jul 12 (CENTCOM's first-ever use of one-way attack drones in this campaign) and a Jul 13 Trump threat to reinstate a Hormuz oil-shipping blockade. This is US-attributable interstate conduct, logged for the digest under United States conduct (composite 17.5, Critical band) -- NOT scored against Iran. The United States was not among tonight's 15 assessed entities; flagged as a candidate for a future priority-cluster assessment if the pattern continues. CONFIRM Iran 2.5, strong downward watch.

Venezuela's earthquake death toll (day 20 since the quake) climbed to 4,490 (+~150 from Jul 11's 4,333), but a threshold re-check confirms the climb is continued disaster-scale body recovery -- natural attribution -- not a new discrete own-conduct failure. This window's actual state signal was incremental relief (housing-plot allocations, ~100k US-supported aid kits). The evidenced own-conduct move stays in the low -3s, sub-threshold. CONFIRM 18.0, strong downward watch sustained.

Four floor countries recorded materially reinforcing evidence without any possibility of a numeric move: Israel (Jul 13 strike killed 8 Palestinians incl. a 9-year-old girl; cumulative post-ceasefire toll now exceeds 1,100 killed), Sudan (El Obeid RSF drone-strike toll newly quantified at 45+ civilians over 3 weeks; EU Parliament calls for RSF terrorist listing), Russia (same Jul 2/Jul 6 Ukraine strike campaign; new EU sanctions on six individuals over chemical-weapons development tied to the Navalny death finding), and Yemen (largest-ever ~1,700-1,750-detainee prisoner exchange remains collapsed, no new implementation date).

Near-floor confirmations continue: DRC (2.3, Ebola toll crossed 600 deaths; newly-surfaced compounding factor -- Ituri healthcare workers walked off the job over unpaid wages, threatening response capacity; natural/epidemic attribution, own-conduct aggravators already priced). Remaining Critical-band entities confirm without new discrete step-changes: China (19.5, Ethnic Unity Law and HK prison-rules tightening continue, last pro-democracy party disbanded), Pakistan (17.2, Operation Shaaban toll rises to 117 alleged militants as of Jul 13, security-source-reported/unverified), Nigeria (18.0, WFP warns of imminent food-assistance cuts atop the already-priced famine record), Lebanon (17.2, fresh Jul 10 Israeli drone strikes remain the dominant harm, not Lebanese own conduct; an unconfirmed partial de-escalation signal does not yet offset the pattern), Mali (12.5, JNIM fuel/food blockade continues to cripple Bamako), and Ukraine (50.0, casualties remain Russian-inflicted, scored vs Russia).

Anthropic (59.1) confirmed with the heightened downward watch (set 2026-07-12) sustained -- no new conversion-trigger event this cycle; the China CVERC/NVD "backdoor" allegation remains the same rival-state allegation already held on 07-12, and Anthropic continues to reject it. Alibaba's internal ban on employee use of Anthropic tools (effective Jul 10) is read as a competitive/geopolitical response, not a new safety or disclosure finding.

The Mali (12.5) vs. Burkina Faso (6.3) cross-peer calibration flag -- routed to coordinator level 2026-06-24 -- reaches roughly its **twentieth consecutive day** tonight (Burkina Faso not in today's 15). The Bolivia critical-band calibration flag (opened 2026-07-11) also remains open, not carried tonight. Six false positives were screened at the scanner level (see below). Zero subdimension sidecars were written tonight (zero dimension changes across all 15 entities) and zero rotation-state drift corrections were needed.

## 2026-07-14 -- Tunisia Reaffirmed (Day 5, STILL PENDING) | Sudan Genocide-Markers Milestone (Floor Reinforced) | Mali-Burkina Faso Calibration ~21 Days | 0 New Proposals | 14 Confirmations

### Summary -- 2026-07-14

Zero new change proposals. The one open proposal (Tunisia) is REAFFIRMED for a fifth consecutive cycle: no new dated escalation surfaced beyond the already-reflected Jul 7-8 mass sentencing (21 opposition figures, 12-35yr terms; Rached Ghannouchi 14yr in absentia) and the 62nd UN Human Rights Council session's deep-concern statement (closed Jul 8). The figure (23.8) is unchanged; no duplicate proposal was opened. **The proposal remains `status: "proposed"` and the published Tunisia composite stays at 34.4** (verified directly against `site/src/data/indexes/countries.json`).

Sudan (0.0) recorded tonight's most consequential development: the UN Human Rights Council's Independent International Fact-Finding Mission formally found (Jul 8-9) that RSF mass killings, abductions, and gang rape in El Fasher (6,000+ killed in three days as the city fell in Oct 2025) bear "distinct markers of genocide," and opened an urgent new inquiry into a near-identical siege pattern replicating around El Obeid. This is a grave escalation in international-legal characterization -- and Sudan is already at the harm-flag floor (0.0), so no numeric move is possible. Logged as a significant evidentiary milestone; floor strongly reinforced.

Iran (2.5) presented a sharpened attribution-split test: own-conduct executions/repression (784+ YTD) intensify at a multi-decade high, but near-floor arithmetic (2.5 points to the absolute floor) forecloses any >=5pt move regardless. Separately, US CENTCOM RESUMED the Strait of Hormuz naval blockade from 4pm Jul 14 -- a concrete escalation from prior weeks' fire exchange alone -- amid a third consecutive weekend of US-Iran fire exchange and Trump's same-day proposed-then-reversed 20% cargo-value "guardian" fee. This is US-attributable interstate conduct, logged for the digest under United States conduct (composite 17.5, Critical band) -- NOT scored against Iran. The United States was not among tonight's 15 assessed entities; flagged again as a candidate for a future priority-cluster assessment.

Venezuela's earthquake death toll (day 21 since the quake) held sustained/flat at 4,490 (16,740 injured, 19,500+ still displaced); a threshold re-check confirms no new discrete own-conduct failure (no evidenced aid diversion or responder-access denial). Evidenced own-conduct move stays in the low -3s, sub-threshold. CONFIRM 18.0, strong downward watch sustained.

Three floor countries recorded materially reinforcing evidence without any possibility of a numeric move (beyond Sudan, above): Israel (Jul 14 strikes killed at least 9 incl. a 10-year-old, Jabalia police-post strike killed 7 incl. the police chief; cumulative post-ceasefire toll now exceeds 1,100 killed), Russia (same Jul 2/Jul 6 Ukraine strike campaign; Jul 3 EU sanctions on six individuals over the Navalny chemical-weapons finding remain the operative record), and Yemen (the ~1,728-detainee prisoner exchange remains stalled; the Jul 11 "renewed commitment" statement has not yet translated into implementation).

Near-floor confirmations continue: DRC (2.3, Ebola toll jumped from 600 to 702 confirmed deaths in just two days -- WHO's true-count estimate now runs 4,000-8,000; natural/epidemic attribution, own-conduct aggravators already priced, near-floor arithmetic forecloses a move). Remaining Critical-band entities confirm without new discrete step-changes: China (19.5, Hong Kong arrest warrants/bounties on 15 more overseas activists, Prison Rules tightening), Pakistan (17.2, Operation Shaaban combined toll rises to 125 as of Jul 14, security-source-reported/unverified), Nigeria (18.0, WFP's worst-in-a-decade hunger record remains operative atop the already-priced famine record), Lebanon (17.2, a fresh Israeli drone strike killed 4 incl. a school principal, remains Israel's conduct not Lebanon's own), Mali (12.5, JNIM fuel/food blockade continues to cripple Bamako), and Ukraine (50.0, casualties remain Russian-inflicted, scored vs Russia).

Anthropic (59.1) confirmed with the heightened downward watch (set 2026-07-12) sustained -- no new conversion-trigger event this cycle; the China CVERC/NVD "backdoor" allegation remains the same rival-state allegation already held on 07-12, and Anthropic continues to reject it. A new age/identity-verification privacy provision (effective Jul 8) is protective, not negative.

The Mali (12.5) vs. Burkina Faso (6.3) cross-peer calibration flag -- routed to coordinator level 2026-06-24 -- reaches roughly its **twenty-first consecutive day** tonight (Burkina Faso not in today's 15). The Bolivia critical-band calibration flag (opened 2026-07-11) also remains open, not carried tonight. Six false positives were screened at the scanner level (see below). ## 2026-07-15 -- Eritrea First Individual Assessment (Placeholder -> Evidence-Based Floor) | Sudan El Obeid Inquiry (Floor Reinforced) | Mali-Burkina Faso Calibration ~22 Days | 0 New Proposals | 15 Confirmations

### Summary -- 2026-07-15

Zero new change proposals. The queue is clear -- Tunisia's proposal was founder-approved and applied 2026-07-14 (34.4 -> 23.8), so there is no carry-forward pending item tonight. This is the fourth consecutive night of zero new proposals.

Tonight's headline event is **Eritrea's first-ever individual assessment**. Eritrea's rotation record showed `last_assessed: null` -- its published 0.0 was a bulk-import placeholder that had never been individually reviewed. The first evidence-based assessment lands exactly on the existing floor (0.0), converting the placeholder into an evidence-based record rather than producing a score change. This is the same class of event as Tunisia's 2026-07-10 first assessment (which moved -10.6 points on review), but with the opposite arithmetic outcome -- Eritrea's placeholder happened to already sit at the value the evidence supports. Basis for the floor: a UN Special Rapporteur finding (Apr 2025-Apr 2026 mandate) of "reasonable grounds to believe crimes against humanity continue" (indefinite conscription as enslavement, enforced disappearance); RSF 2026 World Press Freedom Index ranking Eritrea last of 180 for a third consecutive year; no elections since 1993. The sharply elevated Ethiopia-Eritrea interstate war risk over Red Sea port access that partly surfaced Eritrea this cycle was explicitly **NOT scored** -- it is a risk, not a realized event, and is interstate rather than internal own-conduct. No proposal generated or warranted.

El Salvador (15.0) confirmed with a strong downward watch sustained: the constitutional term-limit amendment and Cristosal's forced exile were already priced into the 15.0 baseline applied 2026-07-05; tonight's evidence (140+ defenders fled, Ruth Lopez still imprisoned) is a sub-threshold continuation of the same conduct pattern, not a discrete new >=5pt event. ACC (1.2) and INT (1.6) were freshly corroborated at their already-low values.

Iran (2.5) confirmed with a strong downward watch: own-conduct executions (784+ YTD) sustain the near-floor score; near-floor arithmetic forecloses any >=5pt move. Separately, the US-Iran interstate conflict entered its fifth consecutive day, with the US Hormuz naval blockade active since Jul 14 and Iran retaliating on US bases in Kuwait, Bahrain, and Jordan -- interstate/US-attributable conduct, logged for the digest, NOT scored against Iran.

Sudan (0.0) had its genocide-markers finding (documented 07-14) reinforced by a new UN Fact-Finding Mission inquiry into a strikingly similar siege pattern forming around El Obeid, North Kordofan. Floor cannot move lower; sustained and substantively reinforced.

Four floor entities recorded reinforcing evidence without any possibility of a numeric move: Israel (Jul 13-15 strikes killed ~a dozen incl. 6 police officers in Jabaliya; cumulative post-ceasefire toll now 1,108), Russia (UN records 293 Ukrainian civilians killed in June 2026, a new monthly record), Yemen (73 UN staff remain arbitrarily detained by Houthi authorities), and xAI/Grok (amended deepfake-CSAM complaint adds Stability AI as co-defendant + systemic NCMEC-reporting-failure allegation).

Near-floor/Critical-band confirmations: DRC (2.3, Ebola toll reached 719, up from 600 four days earlier -- disease-attributed), Pakistan (17.2, Operation Shaaban toll ~125 -- security-source-only, unverified), Lebanon (17.2, harm externally-inflicted by Israel), Venezuela (18.0, earthquake toll rose to 4,333 -- disaster-attributed, sub-threshold), Meta Platforms (7.8, $1.4T penalty figure is a demand not an adjudicated finding; Aug 18 Oakland trial is the scoreable trigger), Tunisia (23.8, Jul 8 mass sentencing SUSTAINS -- does not add to -- the downgrade already APPLIED 2026-07-14; re-proposing would double-count), and Cuba (32.8, third grid collapse in nine days, externally-compounded by the US oil blockade).
